Language first, music next. No compromise on it. Language can exist without song but song cannot without the language, just like flowers can exist without garlands but garlands cannot exist without flowers. BTW, In 2012 or 13, when I was doing PhD in Bhagyanagaram, once I went to that walmart-like huge store near GPO in Abids, they played this song, and I was so amazed especially with charanam @ 1:37 and wanted to know which movie or name of this song, so I can later download and add it to my playlist, but I was so helpless because I don't watch movies much, it was tough for me, so I immediately ran to a lady working there before the song ended, and asked from which movie this song was, she didnt know too, so she went and asked 2-3 other girls and told me the title, which I wrote down on a receipt. Then I got home and googled it. I don't think, I liked any new song (new for 2012/13) that much, like how I like Mahagayini Janakamma and Balu gari songs :) That's one memory linked with this song. I loved this song so much and ended up watching the movie only to regret the wastage of my time and peace of mindğŸ˜‚}
